err != nil {\n   998\u2192\t\t\t\tlevel.Error(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"reloadBlocks\", \"err\", err)\n   999\u2192\t\t\t}\n  1000\u2192\t\t\tdb.cmtx.Unlock()\n  1001\u2192\n  1002\u2192\t\t\tselect {\n  1003\u2192\t\t\tcase db.compactc <- struct{}{}:\n  1004\u2192\t\t\tdefault:\n  1005\u2192\t\t\t}\n  1006\u2192\t\t\t// We attempt mmapping of head chunks regularly.\n  1007\u2192\t\t\tdb.head.mmapHeadChunks()\n  1008\u2192\t\tcase <-db.compactc:\n  1009\u2192\t\t\tdb.metrics.compactionsTriggered.Inc()\n  1010\u2192\n  1011\u2192\t\t\tdb.autoCompactMtx.Lock()\n  1012\u2192\t\t\tif db.autoCompact {\n  1013\u2192\t\t\t\tif err := db.Compact(ctx); err != nil {\n  1014\u2192\t\t\t\t\tlevel.Error(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"compaction failed\", \"err\", err)\n  1015\u2192\t\t\t\t\tbackoff = exponential(backoff, 1*time.Second, 1*time.Minute)\n  1016\u2192\t\t\t\t} else {\n  1017\u2192\t\t\t\t\tbackoff = 0\n  1018\u2192\t\t\t\t}\n  1019\u2192\t\t\t} else {\n  1020\u2192\t\t\t\tdb.metrics.compactionsSkipped.Inc()\n  1021\u2192\t\t\t}\n  1022\u2192\t\t\tdb.autoCompactMtx.Unlock()\n  1023\u2192\t\tcase <-db.stopc:\n  1024\u2192\t\t\treturn\n  1025\u2192\t\t}\n  1026\u2192\t}\n  1027\u2192}\n  1028\u2192\n  1029\u2192// Appender opens a new appender against the database.\n  1030\u2192func (db *DB) Appender(ctx context.Context) storage.Appender {\n  1031\u2192\treturn dbAppender{db: db, Appender: db.head.Appender(ctx)}\n  1032\u2192}\n  1033\u2192\n  1034\u2192// ApplyConfig applies a new config to the DB.\n  1035\u2192// Behaviour of 'OutOfOrderTimeWindow' is as follows:\n  1036\u2192// OOO enabled = oooTimeWindow > 0. OOO disabled = oooTimeWindow is 0.\n  1037\u2192// 1) Before: OOO disabled, Now: OOO enabled =>\n  1038\u2192//   - A new WBL is created for the head block.\n  1039\u2192//   - OOO compaction is enabled.\n  1040\u2192//   - Overlapping queries are enabled.\n  1041\u2192//\n  1042\u2192// 2) Before: OOO enabled, Now: OOO enabled =>\n  1043\u2192//   - Only the time window is updated.\n  1044\u2192//\n  1045\u2192// 3) Before: OOO enabled, Now: OOO disabled =>\n  1046\u2192//   - Time Window set to 0. So no new OOO samples will be allowed.\n  1047\u2192//   - OOO WBL will stay and will be eventually cleaned up.\n  1048\u2192//   - OOO Compaction and overlapping queries will remain enabled until a restart or until all OOO samples are compacted.\n  1049\u2192//\n  1050\u2192// 4) Before: OOO disabled, Now: OOO disabled => no-op.\n  1051\u2192func (db *DB) ApplyConfig(conf *config.Config) error {\n  1052\u2192\toooTimeWindow := int64(0)\n  1053\u2192\tif conf.StorageConfig.TSDBConfig != nil {\n  1054\u2192\t\toooTimeWindow = conf.StorageConfig.TSDBConfig.OutOfOrderTimeWindow\n  1055\u2192\t}\n  1056\u2192\tif oooTimeWindow < 0 {\n  1057\u2192\t\toooTimeWindow = 0\n  1058\u2192\t}\n  1059\u2192\n  1060\u2192\t// Create WBL if it was not present and if OOO is enabled with WAL enabled.\n  1061\u2192\tvar wblog *wlog.WL\n  1062\u2192\tvar err error\n  1063\u2192\tswitch {\n  1064\u2192\tcase db.head.wbl != nil:\n  1065\u2192\t\t// The existing WBL from the disk might have been replayed while OOO was disabled.\n  1066\u2192\t\twblog = db.head.wbl\n  1067\u2192\tcase !db.oooWasEnabled.Load() && oooTimeWindow > 0 && db.opts.WALSegmentSize >= 0:\n  1068\u2192\t\tsegmentSize := wlog.DefaultSegmentSize\n  1069\u2192\t\t// Wal is set to a custom size.\n  1070\u2192\t\tif db.opts.WALSegmentSize > 0 {\n  1071\u2192\t\t\tsegmentSize = db.opts.WALSegmentSize\n  1072\u2192\t\t}\n  1073\u2192\t\toooWalDir := filepath.Join(db.dir, wlog.WblDirName)\n  1074\u2192\t\twblog, err = wlog.NewSize(db.logger, db.registerer, oooWalDir, segmentSize, db.opts.WALCompression)\n  1075\u2192\t\tif err != nil {\n  1076\u2192\t\t\treturn err\n  1077\u2192\t\t}\n  1078\u2192\t}\n  1079\u2192\n  1080\u2192\tdb.opts.OutOfOrderTimeWindow = oooTimeWindow\n  1081\u2192\tdb.head.ApplyConfig(conf, wblog)\n  1082\u2192\n  1083\u2192\tif !db.oooWasEnabled.Load() {\n  1084\u2192\t\tdb.oooWasEnabled.Store(oooTimeWindow > 0)\n  1085\u2192\t}\n  1086\u2192\treturn nil\n  1087\u2192}\n  1088\u2192\n  1089\u2192// EnableNativeHistograms enables the native histogram feature.\n  1090\u2192func (db *DB) EnableNativeHistograms() {\n  1091\u2192\tdb.head.EnableNativeHistograms()\n  1092\u2192}\n  1093\u2192\n  1094\u2192// DisableNativeHistograms disables the native histogram feature.\n  1095\u2192func (db *DB) DisableNativeHistograms() {\n  1096\u2192\tdb.head.DisableNativeHistograms()\n  1097\u2192}\n  1098\u2192\n  1099\u2192// dbAppender wraps the DB's head appender and triggers compactions on commit\n  1100\u2192// if necessary.\n  1101\u2192type dbAppender struct {\n  1102\u2192\tstorage.Appender\n  1103\u2192\tdb *DB\n  1104\u2192}\n  1105\u2192\n  1106\u2192var _ storage.GetRef = dbAppender{}\n  1107\u2192\n  1108\u2192func (a dbAppender) GetRef(lset labels.Labels, hash uint64) (storage.SeriesRef, labels.Labels) {\n  1109\u2192\tif g, ok := a.Appender.(storage.GetRef); ok {\n  1110\u2192\t\treturn g.GetRef(lset, hash)\n  1111\u2192\t}\n  1112\u2192\treturn 0, labels.EmptyLabels()\n  1113\u2192}\n  1114\u2192\n  1115\u2192func (a dbAppender) Commit() error {\n  1116\u2192\terr := a.Appender.Commit()\n  1117\u2192\n  1118\u2192\t// We could just run this check every few minutes practically. But for benchmarks\n  1119\u2192\t// and high frequency use cases this is the safer way.\n  1120\u2192\tif a.db.head.compactable() {\n  1121\u2192\t\tselect {\n  1122\u2192\t\tcase a.db.compactc <- struct{}{}:\n  1123\u2192\t\tdefault:\n  1124\u2192\t\t}\n  1125\u2192\t}\n  1126\u2192\treturn err\n  1127\u2192}\n  1128\u2192\n  1129\u2192// Compact data if possible. After successful compaction blocks are reloaded\n  1130\u2192// which will also delete the blocks that fall out of the retention window.\n  1131\u2192// Old blocks are only deleted on reloadBlocks based on the new block's parent information.\n  1132\u2192// See DB.reloadBlocks documentation for further information.\n  1133\u2192func (db *DB) Compact(ctx context.Context) (returnErr error) {\n  1134\u2192\tdb.cmtx.Lock()\n  1135\u2192\tdefer db.cmtx.Unlock()\n  1136\u2192\tdefer func() {\n  1137\u2192\t\tif returnErr != nil && !errors.Is(returnErr, context.Canceled) {\n  1138\u2192\t\t\t// If we got an error because context was canceled then we're most likely\n  1139\u2192\t\t\t// shutting down TSDB and we don't need to report this on metrics\n  1140\u2192\t\t\tdb.metrics.compactionsFailed.Inc()\n  1141\u2192\t\t}\n  1142\u2192\t}()\n  1143\u2192\n  1144\u2192\tlastBlockMaxt := int64(math.MinInt64)\n  1145\u2192\tdefer func() {\n  1146\u2192\t\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti(returnErr)\n  1147\u2192\t\tif err := db.head.truncateWAL(lastBlockMaxt); err != nil {\n  1148\u2192\t\t\terrs.Add(fmt.Errorf(\"WAL truncation in Compact defer: %w\", err))\n  1149\u2192\t\t}\n  1150\u2192\t\treturnErr = errs.Err()\n  1151\u2192\t}()\n  1152\u2192\n  1153\u2192\tstart := time.Now()\n  1154\u2192\t// Check whether we have pending head blocks that are ready to be persisted.\n  1155\u2192\t// They have the highest priority.\n  1156\u2192\tfor {\n  1157\u2192\t\tselect {\n  1158\u2192\t\tcase <-db.stopc:\n  1159\u2192\t\t\treturn nil\n  1160\u2192\t\tdefault:\n  1161\u2192\t\t}\n  1162\u2192\t\tif !db.head.compactable() {\n  1163\u2192\t\t\tbreak\n  1164\u2192\t\t}\n  1165\u2192\t\tmint := db.head.MinTime()\n  1166\u2192\t\tmaxt := rangeForTimestamp(mint, db.head.chunkRange.Load())\n  1167\u2192\n  1168\u2192\t\t// Wrap head into a range that bounds all reads to it.\n  1169\u2192\t\t// We remove 1 millisecond from maxt because block\n  1170\u2192\t\t// intervals are half-open: [b.MinTime, b.MaxTime). But\n  1171\u2192\t\t// chunk intervals are closed: [c.MinTime, c.MaxTime];\n  1172\u2192\t\t// so in order to make sure that overlaps are evaluated\n  1173\u2192\t\t// consistently, we explicitly remove the last value\n  1174\u2192\t\t// from the block interval here.\n  1175\u2192\t\trh := NewRangeHeadWithIsolationDisabled(db.head, mint, maxt-1)\n  1176\u2192\n  1177\u2192\t\t// Compaction runs with isolation disabled, because head.compactable()\n  1178\u2192\t\t// ensures that maxt is more than chunkRange/2 back from now, and\n  1179\u2192\t\t// head.appendableMinValidTime() ensures that no new appends can start within the compaction range.\n  1180\u2192\t\t// We do need to wait for any overlapping appenders that started previously to finish.\n  1181\u2192\t\tdb.head.WaitForAppendersOverlapping(rh.MaxTime())\n  1182\u2192\n  1183\u2192\t\tif err := db.compactHead(rh); err != nil {\n  1184\u2192\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"compact head: %w\", err)\n  1185\u2192\t\t}\n  1186\u2192\t\t// Consider only successful compactions for WAL truncation.\n  1187\u2192\t\tlastBlockMaxt = maxt\n  1188\u2192\t}\n  1189\u2192\n  1190\u2192\t// Clear some disk space before compacting blocks, especially important\n  1191\u2192\t// when Head compaction happened over a long time range.\n  1192\u2192\tif err := db.head.truncateWAL(lastBlockMaxt); err != nil {\n  1193\u2192\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"WAL truncation in Compact: %w\", err)\n  1194\u2192\t}\n  1195\u2192\n  1196\u2192\tcompactionDuration := time.Since(start)\n  1197\u2192\tif compactionDuration.Milliseconds() > db.head.chunkRange.Load() {\n  1198\u2192\t\tlevel.Warn(db.logger).Log(\n  1199\u2192\t\t\t\"msg\", \"Head compaction took longer than the block time range, compactions are falling behind and won't be able to catch up\",\n  1200\u2192\t\t\t\"duration\", compactionDuration.String(),\n  1201\u2192\t\t\t\"block_range\", db.head.chunkRange.Load(),\n  1202\u2192\t\t)\n  1203\u2192\t}\n  1204\u2192\n  1205\u2192\tif lastBlockMaxt != math.MinInt64 {\n  1206\u2192\t\t// The head was compacted, so we compact OOO head as well.\n  1207\u2192\t\tif err := db.compactOOOHead(ctx); err != nil {\n  1208\u2192\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"compact ooo head: %w\", err)\n  1209\u2192\t\t}\n  1210\u2192\t}\n  1211\u2192\n  1212\u2192\treturn db.compactBlocks()\n  1213\u2192}\n  1214\u2192\n  1215\u2192// CompactHead compacts the given RangeHead.\n  1216\u2192func (db *DB) CompactHead(head *RangeHead) error {\n  1217\u2192\tdb.cmtx.Lock()\n  1218\u2192\tdefer db.cmtx.Unlock()\n  1219\u2192\n  1220\u2192\tif err := db.compactHead(head); err != nil {\n  1221\u2192\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"compact head: %w\", err)\n  1222\u2192\t}\n  1223\u2192\n  1224\u2192\tif err := db.head.truncateWAL(head.BlockMaxTime()); err != nil {\n  1225\u2192\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"WAL truncation: %w\", err)\n  1226\u2192\t}\n  1227\u2192\treturn nil\n  1228\u2192}\n  1229\u2192\n  1230\u2192// CompactOOOHead compacts the OOO Head.\n  1231\u2192func (db *DB) CompactOOOHead(ctx context.Context) error {\n  1232\u2192\tdb.cmtx.Lock()\n  1233\u2192\tdefer db.cmtx.Unlock()\n  1234\u2192\n  1235\u2192\treturn db.compactOOOHead(ctx)\n  1236\u2192}\n  1237\u2192\n  1238\u2192func (db *DB) compactOOOHead(ctx context.Context) error {\n  1239\u2192\tif !db.oooWasEnabled.Load() {\n  1240\u2192\t\treturn nil\n  1241\u2192\t}\n  1242\u2192\toooHead, err := NewOOOCompactionHead(ctx, db.head)\n  1243\u2192\tif err != nil {\n  1244\u2192\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"get ooo compaction head: %w\", err)\n  1245\u2192\t}\n  1246\u2192\n  1247\u2192\tulids, err := db.compactOOO(db.dir, oooHead)\n  1248\u2192\tif err != nil {\n  1249\u2192\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"compact ooo head: %w\", err)\n  1250\u2192\t}\n  1251\u2192\tif err := db.reloadBlocks(); err != nil {\n  1252\u2192\t\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti(err)\n  1253\u2192\t\tfor _, uid := range ulids {\n  1254\u2192\t\t\tif errRemoveAll := os.RemoveAll(filepath.Join(db.dir, uid.String())); errRemoveAll != nil {\n  1255\u2192\t\t\t\terrs.Add(errRemoveAll)\n  1256\u2192\t\t\t}\n  1257\u2192\t\t}\n  1258\u2192\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"reloadBlocks blocks after failed compact ooo head: %w\", errs.Err())\n  1259\u2192\t}\n  1260\u2192\n  1261\u2192\tlastWBLFile, minOOOMmapRef := oooHead.LastWBLFile(), oooHead.LastMmapRef()\n  1262\u2192\tif lastWBLFile != 0 || minOOOMmapRef != 0 {\n  1263\u2192\t\tif minOOOMmapRef != 0 {\n  1264\u2192\t\t\t// Ensure that no more queriers are created that will reference chunks we're about to garbage collect.\n  1265\u2192\t\t\t// truncateOOO waits for any existing queriers that reference chunks we're about to garbage collect to\n  1266\u2192\t\t\t// complete before running garbage collection, so we don't need to do that here.\n  1267\u2192\t\t\t//\n  1268\u2192\t\t\t// We take mtx to ensure that Querier() and ChunkQuerier() don't miss blocks: without this, they could\n  1269\u2192\t\t\t// capture the list of blocks before the call to reloadBlocks() above runs, but then capture\n  1270\u2192\t\t\t// lastGarbageCollectedMmapRef after we update it here, and therefore not query either the blocks we've just\n  1271\u2192\t\t\t// written or the head chunks those blocks were created from.\n  1272\u2192\t\t\tdb.mtx.Lock()\n  1273\u2192\t\t\tdb.lastGarbageCollectedMmapRef = minOOOMmapRef\n  1274\u2192\t\t\tdb.mtx.Unlock()\n  1275\u2192\t\t}\n  1276\u2192\n  1277\u2192\t\tif err := db.head.truncateOOO(lastWBLFile, minOOOMmapRef); err != nil {\n  1278\u2192\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"truncate ooo wbl: %w\", err)\n  1279\u2192\t\t}\n  1280\u2192\t}\n  1281\u2192\n  1282\u2192\treturn nil\n  1283\u2192}\n  1284\u2192\n  1285\u2192// compactOOO creates a new block per possible block range in the compactor's directory from the OOO Head given.\n  1286\u2192// Each ULID in the result corresponds to a block in a unique time range.\n  1287\u2192func (db *DB) compactOOO(dest string, oooHead *OOOCompactionHead) (_ []ulid.ULID, err error) {\n  1288\u2192\tstart := time.Now()\n  1289\u2192\n  1290\u2192\tblockSize := oooHead.ChunkRange()\n  1291\u2192\toooHeadMint, oooHeadMaxt := oooHead.MinTime(), oooHead.MaxTime()\n  1292\u2192\tulids := make([]ulid.ULID, 0)\n  1293\u2192\tdefer func() {\n  1294\u2192\t\tif err != nil {\n  1295\u2192\t\t\t// Best effort removal of created block on any error.\n  1296\u2192\t\t\tfor _, uid := range ulids {\n  1297\u2192\t\t\t\t_ = os.RemoveAll(filepath.Join(db.dir, uid.String()))\n  1298\u2192\t\t\t}\n  1299\u2192\t\t}\n  1300\u2192\t}()\n  1301\u2192\n  1302\u2192\tmeta := &BlockMeta{}\n  1303\u2192\tmeta.Compaction.SetOutOfOrder()\n  1304\u2192\tfor t := blockSize * (oooHeadMint / blockSize); t <= oooHeadMaxt; t += blockSize {\n  1305\u2192\t\tmint, maxt := t, t+blockSize\n  1306\u2192\t\t// Block intervals are half-open: [b.MinTime, b.MaxTime). Block intervals are always +1 than the total samples it includes.\n  1307\u2192\t\tuid, err := db.compactor.Write(dest, oooHead.CloneForTimeRange(mint, maxt-1), mint, maxt, meta)\n  1308\u2192\t\tif err != nil {\n  1309\u2192\t\t\treturn nil, err\n  1310\u2192\t\t}\n  1311\u2192\t\tif uid.Compare(ulid.ULID{}) != 0 {\n  1312\u2192\t\t\tulids = append(ulids, uid)\n  1313\u2192\t\t}\n  1314\u2192\t}\n  1315\u2192\n  1316\u2192\tif len(ulids) == 0 {\n  1317\u2192\t\tlevel.Info(db.logger).Log(\n  1318\u2192\t\t\t\"msg\", \"compact ooo head resulted in no blocks\",\n  1319\u2192\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n  1320\u2192\t\t)\n  1321\u2192\t\treturn nil, nil\n  1322\u2192\t}\n  1323\u2192\n  1324\u2192\tlevel.Info(db.logger).Log(\n  1325\u2192\t\t\"msg\", \"out-of-order compaction completed\",\n  1326\u2192\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n  1327\u2192\t\t\"ulids\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", ulids),\n  1328\u2192\t)\n  1329\u2192\treturn ulids, nil\n  1330\u2192}\n  1331\u2192\n  1332\u2192// compactHead compacts the given RangeHead.\n  1333\u2192// The compaction mutex should be held before calling this method.\n  1334\u2192func (db *DB) compactHead(head *RangeHead) error {\n  1335\u2192\tuid, err := db.compactor.Write(db.dir, head, head.MinTime(), head.BlockMaxTime(), nil)\n  1336\u2192\tif err != nil {\n  1337\u2192\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"persist head block: %w\", err)\n  1338\u2192\t}\n  1339\u2192\n  1340\u2192\tif err := db.reloadBlocks(); err != nil {\n  1341\u2192\t\tif errRemoveAll := os.RemoveAll(filepath.Join(db.dir, uid.String())); errRemoveAll != nil {\n  1342\u2192\t\t\treturn tsdb_errors.NewMulti(\n  1343\u2192\t\t\t\tfmt.Errorf(\"reloadBlocks blocks: %w\", err),\n  1344\u2192\t\t\t\tfmt.Errorf(\"delete persisted head block after failed db reloadBlocks:%s: %w\", uid, errRemoveAll),\n  1345\u2192\t\t\t).Err()\n  1346\u2192\t\t}\n  1347\u2192\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"reloadBlocks blocks: %w\", err)\n  1348\u2192\t}\n  1349\u2192\tif err = db.head.truncateMemory(head.BlockMaxTime()); err != nil {\n  1350\u2192\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"head memory truncate: %w\", err)\n  1351\u2192\t}\n  1352\u2192\treturn nil\n  1353\u2192}\n  1354\u2192\n  1355\u2192// compactBlocks compacts all the eligible on-disk blocks.\n  1356\u2192// The compaction mutex should be held before calling this method.\n  1357\u2192func (db *DB) compactBlocks() (err error) {\n  1358\u2192\t// Check for compactions of multiple blocks.\n  1359\u2192\tfor {\n  1360\u2192\t\t// If we have a lot of blocks to compact the whole process might take\n  1361\u2192\t\t// long enough that we end up with a HEAD block that needs to be written.\n  1362\u2192\t\t// Check if that's the case and stop compactions early.\n  1363\u2192\t\tif db.head.compactable() {\n  1364\u2192\t\t\tlevel.Warn(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"aborting block compactions to persit the head block\")\n  1365\u2192\t\t\treturn nil\n  1366\u2192\t\t}\n  1367\u2192\n  1368\u2192\t\tplan, err := db.compactor.Plan(db.dir)\n  1369\u2192\t\tif err != nil {\n  1370\u2192\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"plan compaction: %w\", err)\n  1371\u2192\t\t}\n  1372\u2192\t\tif len(plan) == 0 {\n  1373\u2192\t\t\tbreak\n  1374\u2192\t\t}\n  1375\u2192\n  1376\u2192\t\tselect {\n  1377\u2192\t\tcase <-db.stopc:\n  1378\u2192\t\t\treturn nil\n  1379\u2192\t\tdefault:\n  1380\u2192\t\t}\n  1381\u2192\n  1382\u2192\t\tuid, err := db.compactor.Compact(db.dir, plan, db.blocks)\n  1383\u2192\t\tif err != nil {\n  1384\u2192\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"compact %s: %w\", plan, err)\n  1385\u2192\t\t}\n  1386\u2192\n  1387\u2192\t\tif err := db.reloadBlocks(); err != nil {\n  1388\u2192\t\t\tif err := os.RemoveAll(filepath.Join(db.dir, uid.String())); err != nil {\n  1389\u2192\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"delete compacted block after failed db reloadBlocks:%s: %w\", uid, err)\n  1390\u2192\t\t\t}\n  1391\u2192\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"reloadBlocks blocks: %w\", err)\n  1392\u2192\t\t}\n  1393\u2192\t}\n  1394\u2192\n  1395\u2192\treturn nil\n  1396\u2192}\n  1397\u2192\n  1398\u2192// getBlock iterates a given block range to find a block by a given id.\n  1399\u2192// If found it returns the block itself and a boolean to indicate that it was found.\n  1400\u2192func getBlock(allBlocks []*Block, id ulid.ULID) (*Block, bool) {\n  1401\u2192\tfor _, b := range allBlocks {\n  1402\u2192\t\tif b.Meta().ULID == id {\n  1403\u2192\t\t\treturn b, true\n  1404\u2192\t\t}\n  1405\u2192\t}\n  1406\u2192\treturn nil, false\n  1407\u2192}\n  1408\u2192\n  1409\u2192// reload reloads blocks and truncates the head and its WAL.\n  1410\u2192func (db *DB) reload() error {\n  1411\u2192\tif err := db.reloadBlocks(); err != nil {\n  1412\u2192\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"reloadBlocks: %w\", err)\n  1413\u2192\t}\n  1414\u2192\tmaxt, ok := db.inOrderBlocksMaxTime()\n  1415\u2192\tif !ok {\n  1416\u2192\t\treturn nil\n  1417\u2192\t}\n  1418\u2192\tif err := db.head.Truncate(maxt); err != nil {\n  1419\u2192\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"head truncate: %w\", err)\n  1420\u2192\t}\n  1421\u2192\treturn nil\n  1422\u2192}\n  1423\u2192\n  1424\u2192// reloadBlocks reloads blocks without touching head.\n  1425\u2192// Blocks that are obsolete due to replacement or retention will be deleted.\n  1426\u2192func (db *DB) reloadBlocks() (err error) {\n  1427\u2192\tdefer func() {\n  1428\u2192\t\tif err != nil {\n  1429\u2192\t\t\tdb.metrics.reloadsFailed.Inc()\n  1430\u2192\t\t}\n  1431\u2192\t\tdb.metrics.reloads.Inc()\n  1432\u2192\t}()\n  1433\u2192\n  1434\u2192\t// Now that we reload TSDB every minute, there is high chance for race condition with a reload\n  1435\u2192\t// triggered by CleanTombstones(). We need to lock the reload to avoid the situation where\n  1436\u2192\t// a normal reload and CleanTombstones try to delete the same block.\n  1437\u2192\tdb.mtx.Lock()\n  1438\u2192\tdefer db.mtx.Unlock()\n  1439\u2192\n  1440\u2192\tloadable, corrupted, err := openBlocks(db.logger, db.dir, db.blocks, db.chunkPool)\n  1441\u2192\tif err != nil {\n  1442\u2192\t\treturn err\n  1443\u2192\t}\n  1444\u2192\n  1445\u2192\tdeletableULIDs := db.blocksToDelete(loadable)\n  1446\u2192\tdeletable := make(map[ulid.ULID]*Block, len(deletableULIDs))\n  1447\u2192\n  1448\u2192\t// Mark all parents of loaded blocks as deletable (no matter if they exists). This makes it resilient against the process\n  1449\u2192\t// crashing towards the end of a compaction but before deletions. By doing that, we can pick up the deletion where it left off during a crash.\n  1450\u2192\tfor _, block := range loadable {\n  1451\u2192\t\tif _, ok := deletableULIDs[block.meta.ULID]; ok {\n  1452\u2192\t\t\tdeletable[block.meta.ULID] = block\n  1453\u2192\t\t}\n  1454\u2192\t\tfor _, b := range block.Meta().Compaction.Parents {\n  1455\u2192\t\t\tif _, ok := corrupted[b.ULID]; ok {\n  1456\u2192\t\t\t\tdelete(corrupted, b.ULID)\n  1457\u2192\t\t\t\tlevel.Warn(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Found corrupted block, but replaced by compacted one so it's safe to delete. This should not happen with atomic deletes.\", \"block\", b.ULID)\n  1458\u2192\t\t\t}\n  1459\u2192\t\t\tdeletable[b.ULID] = nil\n  1460\u2192\t\t}\n  1461\u2192\t}\n  1462\u2192\n  1463\u2192\tif len(corrupted) > 0 {\n  1464\u2192\t\t// Corrupted but no child loaded for it.\n  1465\u2192\t\t// Close all new blocks to release the lock for windows.\n  1466\u2192\t\tfor _, block := range loadable {\n  1467\u2192\t\t\tif _, open := getBlock(db.blocks, block.Meta().ULID); !open {\n  1468\u2192\t\t\t\tblock.Close()\n  1469\u2192\t\t\t}\n  1470\u2192\t\t}\n  1471\u2192\t\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti()\n  1472\u2192\t\tfor ulid, err := range corrupted {\n  1473\u2192\t\t\tif err != nil {\n  1474\u2192\t\t\t\terrs.Add(fmt.Errorf(\"corrupted block %s: %w\", ulid.String(), err))\n  1475\u2192\t\t\t}\n  1476\u2192\t\t}\n  1477\u2192\t\treturn errs.Err()\n  1478\u2192\t}\n  1479\u2192\n  1480\u2192\tvar (\n  1481\u2192\t\ttoLoad     []*Block\n  1482\u2192\t\tblocksSize int64\n  1483\u2192\t)\n  1484\u2192\t// All deletable blocks should be unloaded.\n  1485\u2192\t// NOTE: We need to loop through loadable one more time as there might be loadable ready to be removed (replaced by compacted block).\n  1486\u2192\tfor _, block := range loadable {\n  1487\u2192\t\tif _, ok := deletable[block.Meta().ULID]; ok {\n  1488\u2192\t\t\tdeletable[block.Meta().ULID] = block\n  1489\u2192\t\t\tcontinue\n  1490\u2192\t\t}\n  1491\u2192\n  1492\u2192\t\ttoLoad = append(toLoad, block)\n  1493\u2192\t\tblocksSize += block.Size()\n  1494\u2192\t}\n  1495\u2192\tdb.metrics.blocksBytes.Set(float64(blocksSize))\n  1496\u2192\n  1497\u2192\tslices.SortFunc(toLoad, func(a, b *Block) int {\n  1498\u2192\t\tswitch {\n  1499\u2192\t\tcase a.Meta().MinTime < b.Meta().MinTime:\n  1500\u2192\t\t\treturn -1\n  1501\u2192\t\tcase a.Meta().MinTime > b.Meta().MinTime:\n  1502\u2192\t\t\treturn 1\n  1503\u2192\t\tdefault:\n  1504\u2192\t\t\treturn 0\n  1505\u2192\t\t}\n  1506\u2192\t})\n  1507\u2192\n  1508\u2192\t// Swap new blocks first for subsequently created readers to be seen.\n  1509\u2192\toldBlocks := db.blocks\n  1510\u2192\tdb.blocks = toLoad\n  1511\u2192\n  1512\u2192\tblockMetas := make([]BlockMeta, 0, len(toLoad))\n  1513\u2192\tfor _, b := range toLoad {\n  1514\u2192\t\tblockMetas = append(blockMetas, b.Meta())\n  1515\u2192\t}\n  1516\u2192\tif overlaps := OverlappingBlocks(blockMetas); len(overlaps) > 0 {\n  1517\u2192\t\tlevel.Warn(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Overlapping blocks found during reloadBlocks\", \"detail\", overlaps.String())\n  1518\u2192\t}\n  1519\u2192\n  1520\u2192\t// Append blocks to old, deletable blocks, so we can close them.\n  1521\u2192\tfor _, b := range oldBlocks {\n  1522\u2192\t\tif _, ok := deletable[b.Meta().ULID]; ok {\n  1523\u2192\t\t\tdeletable[b.Meta().ULID] = b\n  1524\u2192\t\t}\n  1525\u2192\t}\n  1526\u2192\tif err := db.deleteBlocks(deletable); err != nil {\n  1527\u2192\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"delete %v blocks: %w\", len(deletable), err)\n  1528\u2192\t}\n  1529\u2192\treturn nil\n  1530\u2192}\n  1531\u2192\n  1532\u2192func openBlocks(l log.Logger, dir string, loaded []*Block, chunkPool chunkenc.Pool) (blocks []*Block, corrupted map[ulid.ULID]error, err error) {\n  1533\u2192\tbDirs, err := blockDirs(dir)\n  1534\u2192\tif err != nil {\n  1535\u2192\t\treturn nil, nil, fmt.Errorf(\"find blocks: %w\", err)\n  1536\u2192\t}\n  1537\u2192\n  1538\u2192\tcorrupted = make(map[ulid.ULID]error)\n  1539\u2192\tfor _, bDir := range bDirs {\n  1540\u2192\t\tmeta, _, err := readMetaFile(bDir)\n  1541\u2192\t\tif err != nil {\n  1542\u2192\t\t\tlevel.Error(l).Log(\"msg\", \"Failed to read meta.json for a block during reloadBlocks. Skipping\", \"dir\", bDir, \"err\", err)\n  1543\u2192\t\t\tcontinue\n  1544\u2192\t\t}\n  1545\u2192\n  1546\u2192\t\t// See if we already have the block in memory or open it otherwise.\n  1547\u2192\t\tblock, open := getBlock(loaded, meta.ULID)\n  1548\u2192\t\tif !open {\n  1549\u2192\t\t\tblock, err = OpenBlock(l, bDir, chunkPool)\n  1550\u2192\t\t\tif err != nil {\n  1551\u2192\t\t\t\tcorrupted[meta.ULID] = err\n  1552\u2192\t\t\t\tcontinue\n  1553\u2192\t\t\t}\n  1554\u2192\t\t}\n  1555\u2192\t\tblocks = append(blocks, block)\n  1556\u2192\t}\n  1557\u2192\treturn blocks, corrupted, nil\n  1558\u2192}\n  1559\u2192\n  1560\u2192// DefaultBlocksToDelete returns a filter which decides time based and size based\n  1561\u2192// retention from the options of the db.\n  1562\u2192func DefaultBlocksToDelete(db *DB) BlocksToDeleteFunc {\n  1563\u2192\treturn func(blocks []*Block) map[ulid.ULID]struct{} {\n  1564\u2192\t\treturn deletableBlocks(db, blocks)\n  1565\u2192\t}\n  1566\u2192}\n  1567\u2192\n  1568\u2192// deletableBlocks returns all currently loaded blocks past retention policy or already compacted into a new block.\n  1569\u2192func deletableBlocks(db *DB, blocks []*Block) map[ulid.ULID]struct{} {\n  1570\u2192\tdeletable := make(map[ulid.ULID]struct{})\n  1571\u2192\n  1572\u2192\t// Sort the blocks by time - newest to oldest (largest to smallest timestamp).\n  1573\u2192\t// This ensures that the retentions will remove the oldest  blocks.\n  1574\u2192\tslices.SortFunc(blocks, func(a, b *Block) int {\n  1575\u2192\t\tswitch {\n  1576\u2192\t\tcase b.Meta().MaxTime < a.Meta().MaxTime:\n  1577\u2192\t\t\treturn -1\n  1578\u2192\t\tcase b.Meta().MaxTime > a.Meta().MaxTime:\n  1579\u2192\t\t\treturn 1\n  1580\u2192\t\tdefault:\n  1581\u2192\t\t\treturn 0\n  1582\u2192\t\t}\n  1583\u2192\t})\n  1584\u2192\n  1585\u2192\tfor _, block := range blocks {\n  1586\u2192\t\tif BeyondTimeRetention(db, blocks) {\n  1592\u2192\t\tdeletable[ulid] = struct{}{}\n  1593\u2192\t}\n  1594\u2192\n  1595\u2192\tfor ulid := range BeyondSizeRetention(db, blocks) {\n  1596\u2192\t\tdeletable[ulid] = struct{}{}\n  1597\u2192\t}\n  1598\u2192\n  1599\u2192\treturn deletable\n  1600\u2192}\n  1601\u2192\n  1602\u2192// BeyondTimeRetention returns those blocks which are beyond the time retention\n  1603\u2192// set in the db options.\n  1604\u2192func BeyondTimeRetention(db *DB, blocks []*Block) (deletable map[ulid.ULID]struct{}) {\n  1605\u2192\t// Time retention is disabled or no blocks to work with.\n  1606\u2192\tif len(blocks) == 0 || db.opts.RetentionDuration == 0 {\n  1607\u2192\t\treturn\n  1608\u2192\t}\n  1609\u2192\n  1610\u2192\tdeletable = make(map[ulid.ULID]struct{})\n  1611\u2192\tfor i, block := range blocks {\n  1612\u2192\t\t// The difference between the first block and this block is greater than or equal to\n  1613\u2192\t\t// the retention period so any blocks after that are added as deletable.\n  1614\u2192\t\tif i > 0 && blocks[0].Meta().MaxTime-block.Meta().MaxTime >= db.opts.RetentionDuration {\n  1615\u2192\t\t\tfor _, b := range blocks[i:] {\n  1616\u2192\t\t\t\tdeletable[b.meta.ULID] = struct{}{}\n  1617\u2192\t\t\t}\n  1618\u2192\t\t\tdb.metrics.timeRetentionCount.Inc()\n  1619\u2192\t\t\tbreak\n  1620\u2192\t\t}\n  1621\u2192\t}\n  1622\u2192\treturn deletable\n  1623\u2192}\n  1624\u2192\n  1625\u2192// BeyondSizeRetention returns those blocks which are beyond the size retention\n  1626\u2192// set in the db options.\n  1627\u2192func BeyondSizeRetention(db *DB, blocks []*Block) (deletable map[ulid.ULID]struct{}) {\n  1628\u2192\t// Size retention is disabled or no blocks to work with.\n  1629\u2192\tif len(blocks) == 0 || db.opts.MaxBytes <= 0 {\n  1630\u2192\t\treturn\n  1631\u2192\t}\n  1632\u2192\n  1633\u2192\tdeletable = make(map[ulid.ULID]struct{})\n  1634\u2192\n  1635\u2192\t// Initializing size counter with WAL size and Head chunks\n  1636\u2192\t// written to disk, as that is part of the retention strategy.\n  1637\u2192\tblocksSize := db.Head().Size()\n  1638\u2192\tfor i, block := range blocks {\n  1639\u2192\t\tblocksSize += block.Size()\n  1640\u2192\t\tif blocksSize > db.opts.MaxBytes {\n  1641\u2192\t\t\t// Add this and all following blocks for deletion.\n  1642\u2192\t\t\tfor _, b := range blocks[i:] {\n  1643\u2192\t\t\t\tdeletable[b.meta.ULID] = struct{}{}\n  1644\u2192\t\t\t}\n  1645\u2192\t\t\tdb.metrics.sizeRetentionCount.Inc()\n  1646\u2192\t\t\tbreak\n  1647\u2192\t\t}\n  1648\u2192\t}\n  1649\u2192\treturn deletable\n  1650\u2192}\n  1651\u2192\n  1652\u2192// deleteBlocks closes the block if loaded and deletes blocks from the disk if exists.\n  1653\u2192// When the map contains a non nil block object it means it is loaded in memory\n  1654\u2192// so needs to be closed first as it might need to wait for pending readers to complete.\n  1655\u2192func (db *DB) deleteBlocks(blocks map[ulid.ULID]*Block) error {\n  1656\u2192\tfor ulid, block := range blocks {\n  1657\u2192\t\tif block != nil {\n  1658\u2192\t\t\tif err := block.Close(); err != nil {\n  1659\u2192\t\t\t\tlevel.Warn(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Closing block failed\", \"err\", err, \"block\", ulid)\n  1660\u2192\t\t\t}\n  1661\u2192\t\t}\n  1662\u2192\n  1663\u2192\t\ttoDelete := filepath.Join(db.dir, ulid.String())\n  1664\u2192\t\tswitch _, err := os.Stat(toDelete); {\n  1665\u2192\t\tcase os.IsNotExist(err):\n  1666\u2192\t\t\t// Noop.\n  1667\u2192\t\t\tcontinue\n  1668\u2192\t\tcase err != nil:\n  1669\u2192\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"stat dir %v: %w\", toDelete, err)\n  1670\u2192\t\t}\n  1671\u2192\n  1672\u2192\t\t// Replace atomically to avoid partial block when process would crash during deletion.\n  1673\u2192\t\ttmpToDelete := filepath.Join(db.dir, fmt.Sprintf(\"%s%s\", ulid, tmpForDeletionBlockDirSuffix))\n  1674\u2192\t\tif err := fileutil.Replace(toDelete, tmpToDelete); err != nil {\n  1675\u2192\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"replace of obsolete block for deletion %s: %w\", ulid, err)\n  1676\u2192\t\t}\n  1677\u2192\t\tif err := os.RemoveAll(tmpToDelete); err != nil {\n  1678\u2192\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"delete obsolete block %s: %w\", ulid, err)\n  1679\u2192\t\t}\n  1680\u2192\t\tlevel.Info(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Deleting obsolete block\", \"block\", ulid)\n  1681\u2192\t}\n  1682\u2192\n  1683\u2192\treturn nil\n  1684\u2192}\n  1685\u2192\n  1686\u2192// TimeRange specifies minTime and maxTime range.\n  1687\u2192type TimeRange struct {\n  1688\u2192\tMin, Max int64\n  1689\u2192}\n  1690\u2192\n  1691\u2192// Overlaps contains overlapping blocks aggregated by overlapping range.\n  1692\u2192type Overlaps map[TimeRange][]BlockMeta\n  1693\u2192\n  1694\u2192// String returns human readable string form of overlapped blocks.\n  1695\u2192func (o Overlaps) String() string {\n  1696\u2192\tvar res []string\n  1697\u2192\tfor r, overlaps := range o {\n  1698\u2192\t\tvar groups []string\n  1699\u2192\t\tfor _, m := range overlaps {\n  1700\u2192\t\t\tgroups = append(groups, fmt.Sprintf(\n  1701\u2192\t\t\t\t\"<ulid: %s, mint: %d, maxt: %d, range: %s>\",\n  1702\u2192\t\t\t\tm.ULID.String(),\n  1703\u2192\t\t\t\tm.MinTime,\n  1704\u2192\t\t\t\tm.MaxTime,\n  1705\u2192\t\t\t\t(time.Duration((m.MaxTime-m.MinTime)/1000)*time.Second).String(),\n  1706\u2192\t\t\t))\n  1707\u2192\t\t}\n  1708\u2192\t\tres = append(res, fmt.Sprintf(\n  1709\u2192\t\t\t\"[mint: %d, maxt: %d, range: %s, blocks: %d]: %s\",\n  1710\u2192\t\t\tr.Min, r.Max,\n  1711\u2192\t\t\t(time.Duration((r.Max-r.Min)/1000)*time.Second).String(),\n  1712\u2192\t\t\tlen(overlaps),\n  1713\u2192\t\t\tstrings.Join(groups, \", \")),\n  1714\u2192\t\t)\n  1715\u2192\t}\n  1716\u2192\treturn strings.Join(res, \"\\n\")\n  1717\u2192}\n  1718\u2192\n  1719\u2192// OverlappingBlocks returns all overlapping blocks from given meta files.\n  1720\u2192func OverlappingBlocks(bm []BlockMeta) Overlaps {\n  1721\u2192\tif len(bm) <= 1 {\n  1722\u2192\t\treturn nil\n  1723\u2192\t}\n  1724\u2192\tvar (\n  1725\u2192\t\toverlaps [][]BlockMeta\n  1726\u2192\n  1727\u2192\t\t// pending contains not ended blocks in regards to \"current\" timestamp.\n  1728\u2192\t\tpending = []BlockMeta{bm[0]}\n  1729\u2192\t\t// continuousPending helps to aggregate same overlaps to single group.\n  1730\u2192\t\tcontinuousPending = true\n  1731\u2192\t)\n  1732\u2192\n  1733\u2192\t// We have here blocks sorted by minTime. We iterate over each block and treat its minTime as our \"current\" timestamp.\n  1734\u2192\t// We check if any of the pending block finished (blocks that we have seen before, but their maxTime was still ahead current\n  1735\u2192\t// timestamp). If not, it means they overlap with our current block. In the same time current block is assumed pending.\n  1736\u2192\tfor _, b := range bm[1:] {\n  1737\u2192\t\tvar newPending []BlockMeta\n  1738\u2192\n  1739\u2192\t\tfor _, p := range pending {\n  1740\u2192\t\t\t// \"b.MinTime\" is our current time.\n  1741\u2192\t\t\tif b.MinTime >= p.MaxTime {\n  1742\u2192\t\t\t\tcontinuousPending = false\n  1743\u2192\t\t\t\tcontinue\n  1744\u2192\t\t\t}\n  1745\u2192\n  1746\u2192\t\t\t// \"p\" overlaps with \"b\" and \"p\" is still pending.\n  1747\u2192\t\t\tnewPending = append(newPending, p)\n  1748\u2192\t\t}\n  1749\u2192\n  1750\u2192\t\t// Our block \"b\" is now pending.\n  1751\u2192\t\tpending = append(newPending, b)\n  1752\u2192\t\tif len(newPending) == 0 {\n  1753\u2192\t\t\t// No overlaps.\n  1754\u2192\t\t\tcontinue\n  1755\u2192\t\t}\n  1756\u2192\n  1757\u2192\t\tif continuousPending && len(overlaps) > 0 {\n  1758\u2192\t\t\toverlaps[len(overlaps)-1] = append(overlaps[len(overlaps)-1], b)\n  1759\u2192\t\t\tcontinue\n  1760\u2192\t\t}\n  1761\u2192\t\toverlaps = append(overlaps, append(newPending, b))\n  1762\u2192\t\t// Start new pendings.\n  1763\u2192\t\tcontinuousPending = true\n  1764\u2192\t}\n  1765\u2192\n  1766\u2192\t// Fetch the critical overlapped time range foreach overlap groups.\n  1767\u2192\toverlapGroups := Overlaps{}\n  1768\u2192\tfor _, overlap := range overlaps {\n  1769\u2192\t\tminRange := TimeRange{Min: 0, Max: math.MaxInt64}\n  1770\u2192\t\tfor _, b := range overlap {\n  1771\u2192\t\t\tif minRange.Max > b.MaxTime {\n  1772\u2192\t\t\t\tminRange.Max = b.MaxTime\n  1773\u2192\t\t\t}\n  1774\u2192\n  1775\u2192\t\t\tif minRange.Min < b.MinTime {\n  1776\u2192\t\t\t\tminRange.Min = b.MinTime\n  1777\u2192\t\t\t}\n  1778\u2192\t\t}\n  1779\u2192\t\toverlapGroups[minRange] = overlap\n  1780\u2192\t}\n  1781\u2192\n  1782\u2192\treturn overlapGroups\n  1783\u2192}\n  1784\u2192\n  1785\u2192func (db *DB) String() string {\n  1786\u2192\treturn \"HEAD\"\n  1787\u2192}\n  1788\u2192\n  1789\u2192// Blocks returns the databases persisted blocks.\n  1790\u2192func (db *DB) Blocks() []*Block {\n  1791\u2192\tdb.mtx.RLock()\n  1792\u2192\tdefer db.mtx.RUnlock()\n  1793\u2192\n  1794\u2192\treturn db.blocks\n  1795\u2192}\n  1796\u2192\n  1797\u2192// inOrderBlocksMaxTime returns the max time among the blocks that were not totally created\n  1798\u2192// out of out-of-order data. If the returned boolean is true, it means there is at least\n  1799\u2192// one such block.\n  1800\u2192func (db *DB) inOrderBlocksMaxTime() (maxt int64, ok bool) {\n  1801\u2192\tmaxt, ok = int64(math.MinInt64), false\n  1802\u2192\t// If blocks are overlapping, last block might not have the max time. So check all blocks.\n  1803\u2192\tfor _, b := range db.Blocks() {\n  1804\u2192\t\tif !b.meta.Compaction.FromOutOfOrder() && b.meta.MaxTime > maxt {\n  1805\u2192\t\t\tok = true\n  1806\u2192\t\t\tmaxt = b.meta.MaxTime\n  1807\u2192\t\t}\n  1808\u2192\t}\n  1809\u2192\treturn maxt, ok\n  1810\u2192}\n  1811\u2192\n  1812\u2192// Head returns the databases's head.\n  1813\u2192func (db *DB) Head() *Head {\n  1814\u2192\treturn db.head\n  1815\u2192}\n  1816\u2192\n  1817\u2192// Close the partition.\n  1818\u2192func (db *DB) Close() error {\n  1819\u2192\tclose(db.stopc)\n  1820\u2192\tif db.compactCancel != nil {\n  1821\u2192\t\tdb.compactCancel()\n  1822\u2192\t}\n  1823\u2192\t<-db.donec\n  1824\u2192\n  1825\u2192\tdb.mtx.Lock()\n  1826\u2192\tdefer db.mtx.Unlock()\n  1827\u2192\n  1828\u2192\tvar g errgroup.Group\n  1829\u2192\n  1830\u2192\t// blocks also contains all head blocks.\n  1831\u2192\tfor _, pb := range db.blocks {\n  1832\u2192\t\tg.Go(pb.Close)\n  1833\u2192\t}\n  1834\u2192\n  1835\u2192\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti(g.Wait(), db.locker.Release())\n  1836\u2192\tif db.head != nil {\n  1837\u2192\t\terrs.Add(db.head.Close())\n  1838\u2192\t}\n  1839\u2192\treturn errs.Err()\n  1840\u2192}\n  1841\u2192\n  1842\u2192// DisableCompactions disables auto compactions.\n  1843\u2192func 1848\u2192\tlevel.Info(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Compactions disabled\")\n  1849\u2192}\n  1850\u2192\n  1851\u2192// EnableCompactions enables auto compactions.\n  1852\u2192func (db *DB) 30. Write @ -
Input
{
  "content": "# Prometheus TSDB Compaction Operational Runbook\n\n## 1. Overview\n\n### Purpose of Compaction\n\nTSDB (Time Series Database) compaction in Prometheus serves three critical functions:\n\n1. **Block Consolidation**: Merges overlapping time blocks to reduce the number of files that need to be queried\n2. **Tombstone Cleanup**: Physically removes series marked for deletion by applying tombstone metadata, reducing disk footprint\n3. **Query Performance**: Maintains optimal query performance by keeping block sizes and levels balanced according to exponential growth\n\nWithout compaction, Prometheus would accumulate small blocks indefinitely, degrading query performance and consuming excessive disk space. Compaction is triggered automatically by Prometheus and typically requires no manual intervention.\n\n### Block Structure and Compaction Levels\n\n**Block Basics**:\n- Each block represents a time-ordered chunk of time series data\n- Blocks have half-open time intervals: `[MinTime, MaxTime)` where MaxTime is exclusive\n- Block structure includes: chunks (samples), index (series metadata), tombstones (deletion markers), meta.json (metadata)\n- Block identifiers are ULIDs (Universally Unique Lexicographically Sortable Identifiers)\n\n**Compaction Levels**:\nPrometheus uses exponential block ranges to organize blocks hierarchically. Given default configuration:\n- **Level 0** (Head blocks): ~2 hours of data from active writes\n- **Level 1**: Result of compacting Level 0 blocks (~6 hours = 3 \u00d7 2h)\n- **Level 2**: Result of compacting Level 1 blocks (~18 hours = 3 \u00d7 6h)\n- **Level 3+**: Continue exponential growth with factor of 3\n\nThis is configured via `DefaultBlockDuration` (2 hours) and exponential step factor (3) in `tsdb/db.go:745-749`.\n\n**Block Metadata Tracking**:\nEach compacted block includes:\n- `Compaction.Level`: How many times this block has been compacted (0=fresh head, 1+=compacted blocks)\n- `Compaction.Sources`: All original head block ULIDs merged into this block\n- `Compaction.Parents`: Direct parent blocks (for tracking lineage during compaction failures)\n- `Compaction.Failed`: Flag indicating if compaction failed (prevents future selection)\n\n### When Compaction is Triggered\n\nCompaction occurs through three independent mechanisms:\n\n#### 1. Head Block Compaction (Time-Based)\n**Condition**: When `(MaxTime - MinTime) > (ChunkRange / 2) * 3` (approximately 3 hours with default 2h chunk range)\n\n**Code Location**: `tsdb/head.go:1630-1639` (`Head.compactable()` method)\n\n**Trigger Pathway**:\n- Periodic check every ~1 minute (DB reload loop in `tsdb/db.go:982-1027`)\n- On-commit signal when samples are appended (`tsdb/db.go:1115-1127`)\n\nWhen the head block meets this threshold, it becomes compactable and will be persisted to disk during the next `DB.Compact()` call.\n\n#### 2. Block-to-Block Compaction (Leveled)\n**Condition**: Multiple blocks at the same compaction level that fit exponential bucket requirements\n\n**Code Location**: `tsdb/compact.go:242-338` (`LeveledCompactor.plan()` method)\n\n**Selection Logic**:\n- Identifies overlapping blocks first (vertical compaction)\n- For non-overlapping blocks: groups by time range and compacts full exponential levels\n- Skips blocks with previous compaction failures (marked `Compaction.Failed = true`)\n- Always excludes the most recent block (preserves write window)\n\n#### 3. Tombstone Cleanup Compaction\n**Condition**: Blocks with >5% of samples deleted via tombstones\n\n**Code Location**: `tsdb/compact.go:302-315` (tombstone selection logic)\n\nPeriodically triggered via `DB.CleanTombstones()` to reclaim disk space from deleted series.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Key Prometheus Metrics\n\nThe following metrics are emitted by the LeveledCompactor and should be monitored continuously. All metrics are registered in `tsdb/compact.go:99-151` (`NewCompactorMetrics()` function).\n\n#### Counter Metrics\n\n**`prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total`**\n- Type: Counter\n- Meaning: Total number of compactions executed (both successful and failed ones that were marked)\n- Alert if: Stopped incrementing for >5 minutes despite active time series writes\n- Indicates: Head blocks are not becoming compactable; potential data accumulation\n\n**`prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total`**\n- Type: Counter\n- Meaning: Number of compactions where overlapping blocks were detected and merged\n- Alert if: Continuously increasing rapidly (>10/minute) indicating chronic overlap\n- Indicates: Block generation may be overlapping more than expected (potential for stuck compaction)\n\n#### Gauge Metrics\n\n**`prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block`**\n- Type: Gauge (0 or 1)\n- Meaning: Set to 1 when actively writing compacted data to disk, 0 otherwise\n- Alert if: Remains 1 for >10 minutes (indicates stuck compaction)\n- Indicates: Compaction write operation is hanging, likely I/O or memory issue\n\n#### Histogram Metrics\n\n**`prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds`**\n- Type: Histogram with exponential buckets (1s to 16384s)\n- Meaning: Wall-clock time to complete a compaction operation\n- Alert if: P99 percentile >5 minutes OR regularly hitting the largest bucket\n- Indicates: System is I/O bound or under memory pressure during compaction\n\n**`prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_size_bytes`**\n- Type: Histogram\n- Meaning: Final byte size of chunks after first-level compaction\n- Alert if: P95 percentile >1MB (indicates potential compression issues)\n- Indicates: Chunks are larger than expected; may affect memory usage\n\n**`prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_samples`**\n- Type: Histogram\n- Meaning: Number of samples per chunk after first-level compaction\n- Alert if: P95 percentile >5000 (typical is 500-2000)\n- Indicates: High-cardinality or high-resolution data; normal for certain workloads\n\n**`prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_range_seconds`**\n- Type: Histogram\n- Meaning: Time range covered per chunk after compaction\n- Alert if: P95 percentile significantly <7200s (2 hours), indicating early chunk boundary crossing\n- Indicates: Chunks may be too granular; query performance could be affected\n\n### Related Database Metrics\n\nMonitor alongside compaction metrics:\n\n**`prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded`**\n- Number of currently loaded blocks; should be relatively stable\n- Increase during compaction (new blocks loaded), then decrease (old blocks deleted)\n- Alert if: Remains elevated after compaction completes (failed cleanup)\n\n**`prometheus_tsdb_block_truncations_total`**\n- Blocks deleted due to retention settings\n- Should increase as data cycles through retention period\n\n**`prometheus_tsdb_reloads_total`**\n- Block reloads triggered (typically 1 per minute)\n- Increases after each compaction cycle\n\n**`prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total`**\n- Failed block reload attempts\n- Alert if: Increases; indicates compacted blocks cannot be loaded\n\n### Distinguishing Healthy vs. Stuck Compaction\n\n**Healthy Compaction Pattern**:\n```\n1. prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total increments\n2. prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block \u2192 1 (for <2 minutes)\n3. prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds records value (1-300s typical)\n4. prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block \u2192 0\n5. prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded momentarily increases, then stabilizes\n6. Repeat every 5-15 minutes during write load\n```\n\n**Stuck Compaction Pattern**:\n```\n1. prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block = 1 (for >10 minutes)\n2. prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds histogram stops recording\n3. prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded increasing or high volatility\n4. prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total increments\n5. Prometheus memory/CPU usage elevated\n6. No new compactions_total increments\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Symptoms**:\n- Compaction progress halts; `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1\n- Error logs: \"no space left on device\" or \"ENOSPC\"\n- New blocks fail to be created (`.tmp-for-creation` directory cannot be written)\n- Prometheus memory grows as head block accumulates uncompacted data\n- Query latency increases\n\n**Likely Causes**:\n- Retention policy not aggressive enough for ingestion rate\n- Unexpected spike in sample ingestion\n- Compacted blocks not properly cleaned up (parents not deleted)\n- `.tmp-for-deletion` or `.tmp-for-creation` directories persist from crashed compaction\n\n**Diagnostic Steps**:\n\n1. Check available disk space:\n   ```bash\n   df -h /path/to/prometheus/data\n   du -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/*\n   ```\n\n2. Identify largest blocks:\n   ```bash\n   cd /path/to/prometheus/data && du -sh */ | sort -rh | head -10\n   ```\n\n3. Check for orphaned temporary directories:\n   ```bash\n   ls -la /path/to/prometheus/data | grep \"tmp-\"\n   ```\n\n4. Examine Prometheus logs for recent compaction attempts:\n   ```bash\n   grep -E \"(compaction|failed)\" /path/to/prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n5. List blocks and check metadata using promtool:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/data\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure**:\n\n1. **Increase disk space immediately** (add more storage to the mounted filesystem)\n\n2. **Clean up orphaned temporary directories**:\n   ```bash\n   rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/*.tmp-for-creation\n   rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/*.tmp-for-deletion\n   ```\n\n3. **Delete old blocks exceeding retention** (if aggressive cleanup is safe):\n   ```bash\n   # Identify minimum block time to keep (e.g., 7 days ago in milliseconds)\n   MIN_TIME=$(($(date +%s) - 7*24*3600))000\n\n   for blockdir in /path/to/prometheus/data/*/; do\n     ULID=$(basename \"$blockdir\")\n     # Extract timestamp from ULID (first 10 characters = timestamp in 10ms units)\n     BLOCKTIME=$((16#${ULID:0:8} * 1000))\n     if [ $BLOCKTIME -lt $MIN_TIME ]; then\n       rm -rf \"$blockdir\"\n     fi\n   done\n   ```\n\n4. **Trigger compaction manually** (if Prometheus is still running):\n   ```bash\n   # Use Prometheus HTTP API if available\n   curl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/clean-tombstones\n   ```\n\n5. **If necessary, stop Prometheus and compact externally**:\n   ```bash\n   # Stop Prometheus\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n\n   # Wait for graceful shutdown (~30s)\n\n   # Trigger manual compaction (if Prometheus has built-in CLI support)\n   # Or restart to allow normal compaction\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n6. **Monitor recovery**:\n   ```bash\n   # Watch disk usage decrease\n   watch -n 5 \"du -sh /path/to/prometheus/data\"\n\n   # Monitor compaction metric\n   curl http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total\n   ```\n\n7. **Adjust retention policy** to prevent recurrence:\n   ```yaml\n   # In prometheus.yml\n   global:\n     retention: \"15d\"      # or reduce if disk-constrained\n     retention_size: \"50GB\"  # hard limit on storage\n   ```\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n**Symptoms**:\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block = 1` for extended period (>10 minutes)\n- No new `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` increments\n- Head blocks accumulating without being persisted\n- Prometheus memory usage climbing (uncompacted head data)\n- Query latency degrading over time\n\n**Likely Causes**:\n- Deadlock in compaction mutex (`cmtx`) due to concurrent compaction and query\n- Hung I/O operation (slow disk, NFS timeout, filesystem fsck)\n- Out-of-memory condition killing compaction goroutine\n- Context cancellation not properly handled\n- Corrupted block preventing reload (blocks loading after compaction fails)\n\n**Diagnostic Steps**:\n\n1. Check if Prometheus is responsive to queries:\n   ```bash\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=up | head -20\n   ```\n\n2. Monitor current goroutines and memory:\n   ```bash\n   # Check process status\n   ps aux | grep prometheus\n\n   # Check memory/CPU\n   top -p <prometheus-pid>\n\n   # Get goroutine count and memory via pprof\n   curl http://localhost:6060/debug/pprof/goroutine | grep \"goroutine\"\n   curl http://localhost:6060/debug/pprof/heap | grep \"alloc_space\"\n   ```\n\n3. Check filesystem I/O:\n   ```bash\n   # Monitor I/O on Prometheus data directory\n   iotop -o -k -p <prometheus-pid>\n\n   # Check for stuck I/O operations\n   lsof -p <prometheus-pid> | grep prometheus/data\n   ```\n\n4. Examine Prometheus logs for context cancellation or blocked goroutines:\n   ```bash\n   tail -f /path/to/prometheus.log | grep -i -E \"(compact|context|cancel|deadline)\"\n   ```\n\n5. Use pprof to capture goroutine dump:\n   ```bash\n   curl http://localhost:6060/debug/pprof/goroutine?debug=2 > /tmp/goroutine.txt\n   grep -A 20 \"compactBlocks\\|compactHead\\|Compact\" /tmp/goroutine.txt\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure**:\n\n1. **Try graceful shutdown first** (signals may unblock I/O):\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   # Wait up to 120 seconds for shutdown\n   sleep 120\n   ```\n\n2. **If Prometheus is hung**, use kill signal:\n   ```bash\n   # SIGTERM (graceful)\n   kill -TERM <prometheus-pid>\n   sleep 30\n\n   # SIGKILL (forced) if SIGTERM doesn't work\n   kill -9 <prometheus-pid>\n   ```\n\n3. **Restart Prometheus**:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n4. **Monitor compaction after restart**:\n   ```bash\n   # Watch for compaction progress\n   watch -n 2 \"curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total | grep -o '\\\"value\\\":\\[[^]]*' | tail -1\"\n\n   # Monitor memory growth\n   watch -n 5 \"ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\"\n   ```\n\n5. **If compaction still stuck after restart**:\n   - Check for corrupted blocks (see Failure Mode 3)\n   - Manually remove recently compacted blocks if they cannot be loaded:\n     ```bash\n     systemctl stop prometheus\n     # Remove blocks created in last 1 hour\n     find /path/to/prometheus/data -name \"meta.json\" -mmin -60 -print0 | xargs -0 dirname | xargs rm -rf\n     systemctl start prometheus\n     ```\n\n6. **Check for OOM condition** (see Failure Mode 4):\n   ```bash\n   dmesg | grep -E \"(Killed|OOM|memory)\" | tail -20\n   ```\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n**Symptoms**:\n- Errors in logs: \"block corrupted\", \"invalid block\", \"index corrupted\", \"chunk corruption detected\"\n- `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` increments\n- Queries return errors or unexpected results from specific time ranges\n- Compaction cannot proceed because corrupted block cannot be loaded\n- Block appears in `promtool list` but `promtool analyze` fails\n\n**Likely Causes**:\n- Partial write during compaction (unclean shutdown, process killed mid-write)\n- Disk corruption (bad sectors, filesystem inconsistency)\n- Memory corruption during compaction (rare, but possible with faulty RAM)\n- Index or chunk file truncated or partially overwritten\n- Incompatible Prometheus version writing block that current version cannot read\n\n**Diagnostic Steps**:\n\n1. Identify corrupted block from logs:\n   ```bash\n   grep -i \"corrupted\\|invalid\" /path/to/prometheus.log | head -5\n   # Look for ULID in error message\n   ```\n\n2. Verify block integrity with promtool:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/data\n   # Note which block has issues\n\n   promtool tsdb analyze /path/to/prometheus/data <BLOCK_ULID>\n   ```\n\n3. Check block files directly:\n   ```bash\n   BLOCK_DIR=\"/path/to/prometheus/data/<BLOCK_ULID>\"\n\n   # Verify files exist\n   ls -la \"$BLOCK_DIR\"\n\n   # Check file sizes\n   stat \"$BLOCK_DIR\"/meta.json\n   stat \"$BLOCK_DIR\"/chunks/\n   stat \"$BLOCK_DIR\"/index\n\n   # Check for truncated files (size 0 or much smaller than expected)\n   ```\n\n4. Attempt to dump block contents:\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb dump /path/to/prometheus/data --min-time <START> --max-time <END> > /tmp/dump.txt 2>&1\n   # If dump fails for specific time range, that's where corruption is\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure**:\n\n1. **Stop Prometheus immediately** to prevent further corruption:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   ```\n\n2. **Backup corrupted block before deletion** (for debugging):\n   ```bash\n   cp -r /path/to/prometheus/data/<BLOCK_ULID> /path/to/prometheus/data/<BLOCK_ULID>.backup\n   ```\n\n3. **Delete corrupted block**:\n   ```bash\n   rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/<BLOCK_ULID>\n   ```\n\n4. **Clean up associated temporary directories**:\n   ```bash\n   # If block was being compacted when corruption occurred\n   rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/${BLOCK_ULID}.tmp-for-creation\n   rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/${BLOCK_ULID}.tmp-for-deletion\n   ```\n\n5. **If the corrupted block is a compacted block** (contains parent blocks), delete its parents too:\n   ```bash\n   # Extract metadata to find parent ULIDs\n   cat /path/to/prometheus/data/<BLOCK_ULID>.backup/meta.json | jq '.compaction.parents[] | .ulid'\n\n   # Delete each parent\n   rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/<PARENT_ULID>\n   ```\n\n6. **Check and repair filesystem** (if disk corruption suspected):\n   ```bash\n   # Unmount filesystem safely\n   # This requires stopping all services using the mount\n   umount /path/to/prometheus\n\n   # Run filesystem check\n   fsck -n /dev/sdX  # -n for read-only check first\n   fsck -y /dev/sdX  # -y to auto-repair if confident\n\n   # Remount\n   mount /path/to/prometheus\n   ```\n\n7. **Restart Prometheus**:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n8. **Verify recovery**:\n   ```bash\n   # Check that blocks can be reloaded\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded\n\n   # Run queries to verify data availability\n   curl -s 'http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=rate(http_requests_total[5m])' | head -10\n   ```\n\n9. **Monitor for re-corruption** and investigate underlying cause:\n   - Run `memtest` on RAM if memory corruption suspected\n   - Check disk health with `smartctl`\n   - Review Prometheus version compatibility\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n**Symptoms**:\n- Prometheus process exits abruptly with status 137 or 139 (killed by kernel)\n- Logs show \"cannot allocate memory\" or \"OOM killer invoked\"\n- `dmesg` contains \"Killed\" messages for prometheus process\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` never records (process dies mid-compaction)\n- System memory usage spikes to 100% before crash\n- Occurs during specific compaction operations (particularly large blocks)\n\n**Likely Causes**:\n- Insufficient memory for compactor to hold open blocks + merge state\n- Accumulation of many small blocks requiring simultaneous loading\n- Chunk pool exhaustion (chunks not being released properly)\n- Large cardinality spike ingesting many new series\n- Compaction of out-of-order (OOO) blocks requiring extra memory\n- Memory leak in compaction code (rare)\n\n**Diagnostic Steps**:\n\n1. Check available memory before crash:\n   ```bash\n   # Monitor memory during compaction\n   watch -n 1 \"free -h; ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\"\n   ```\n\n2. Check dmesg for OOM killer invocations:\n   ```bash\n   dmesg | grep -i \"oom\\|killed\" | tail -20\n   ```\n\n3. Check Prometheus memory configuration:\n   ```bash\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\n   # Note ulimit settings\n\n   cat /proc/<prometheus-pid>/limits | grep \"memory\"\n   ```\n\n4. Estimate memory needed for compaction:\n   ```bash\n   # Get block directory sizes\n   du -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/*/\n\n   # Typical rule: need (source_block_size * 2) to 3x for merge buffers\n   # Plus heap overhead\n   ```\n\n5. Check for chunk pool exhaustion:\n   ```bash\n   # Look for warnings about chunk pool in logs\n   grep -i \"chunk pool\\|memory\\|alloc\" /path/to/prometheus.log | tail -20\n   ```\n\n**Recovery Procedure**:\n\n1. **Stop Prometheus**:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   ```\n\n2. **Increase available memory** (choose one approach):\n\n   **Option A: Increase system memory** (preferred)\n   - Add RAM to server\n   - May require reboot\n\n   **Option B: Increase swap space** (temporary)\n   ```bash\n   # Create swap file\n   fallocate -l 4G /swapfile\n   chmod 600 /swapfile\n   mkswap /swapfile\n   swapon /swapfile\n\n   # Make permanent\n   echo '/swapfile none swap sw 0 0' >> /etc/fstab\n   ```\n\n   **Option C: Increase JVM/process memory limits**\n   ```bash\n   # Edit systemd service\n   systemctl edit prometheus\n\n   # Add to [Service] section:\n   # MemoryMax=16G\n   # MemoryHigh=14G\n   ```\n\n3. **Reduce write volume** to compaction (reduce retention or increase block duration):\n   ```yaml\n   global:\n     retention: \"7d\"  # Shorter retention = smaller blocks\n\n   # Or increase block duration (restart required)\n   storage:\n     tsdb:\n       max_block_duration: 3h  # Default 2h, increase to reduce block count\n   ```\n\n4. **Manually clean tombstones** to reduce block count:\n   ```bash\n   # Stop Prometheus\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n\n   # This would normally reduce number of blocks via compaction\n   # But we can avoid heavy compaction by manual cleanup\n\n   # Restart\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n5. **Restart Prometheus**:\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n6. **Monitor memory during compaction**:\n   ```bash\n   # In one terminal\n   watch -n 1 \"free -h\"\n\n   # In another terminal\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block\n   ```\n\n7. **If OOM recurs**, reduce ingestion rate:\n   ```yaml\n   # In scrape configs, reduce frequency\n   scrape_interval: 30s  # Default is 15s\n\n   # Or drop high-cardinality metrics\n   metric_relabel_configs:\n     - source_labels: [__name__]\n       regex: 'high_cardinality_metric_.*'\n       action: drop\n   ```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures Summary Table\n\n| Failure Mode | Primary Symptom | Quick Diagnosis | Immediate Action | Full Recovery |\n|---|---|---|---|---|\n| Disk Full | ENOSPC errors | `df -h /path/to/prometheus/data` | Add storage OR delete temp dirs | Clean old blocks, adjust retention |\n| Stuck Compaction | `compaction_populating_block=1` for >10min | `curl prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Restart Prometheus | Check for I/O hangs, corrupted blocks |\n| Block Corruption | \"invalid block\" in logs | `promtool tsdb analyze` | Stop Prometheus, delete block | Rebuild from backup, check filesystem |\n| OOM Killer | Process exits 137, dmesg OOM | `free -h; dmesg \\| grep -i oom` | Add swap OR restart | Increase memory, reduce retention |\n\n---\n\n## 5. Code References\n\n### Critical Functions by Failure Mode\n\n**Compaction Triggering & Planning** (`tsdb/compact.go`):\n- `LeveledCompactor.Plan()` at lines 222-240: Identifies which blocks to compact\n- `LeveledCompactor.plan()` at lines 242-338: Internal planning logic, checks for overlaps and failures\n- `LeveledCompactor.selectDirs()` at lines 342-380: Selects non-overlapping blocks for compaction\n- `LeveledCompactor.selectOverlappingDirs()` at lines 385-415: Identifies overlapping blocks\n\n**Compaction Execution** (`tsdb/compact.go`):\n- `LeveledCompactor.Compact()` at lines 444-537: Main compaction entry point\n- `LeveledCompactor.write()` at lines 607-718: Persists compacted block to disk\n- `DefaultBlockPopulator.PopulateBlock()` at lines 729-875: Merges series and chunks from source blocks\n\n**Error Handling** (`tsdb/compact.go`):\n- Lines 527-535: Sets `CompactionFailed` flag when compaction fails (prevents re-selection)\n- Line 616: Cleans up `.tmp-for-creation` directory on write failure\n\n**Head Compaction Triggering** (`tsdb/head.go`):\n- `Head.compactable()` at lines 1630-1639: Determines when head block is ready to persist\n\n**Database Compaction Orchestration** (`tsdb/db.go`):\n- `DB.Compact()` at lines 1133-1213: Main compaction orchestrator, triggers head then block compaction\n- `DB.compactHead()` at lines 1216-1229: Persists head block\n- `DB.compactBlocks()` at lines 1357-1396: Compacts persisted blocks in a loop\n- `DB.reloadBlocks()` at lines 1426-1500: Loads newly compacted blocks and deletes old ones\n- `DB.blocksToDelete()` at lines 1502-1569: Determines which blocks are obsolete\n- Lines 1440-1443: `openBlocks()` detects corrupted blocks and returns them separately\n\n**Tombstone Cleanup** (`tsdb/db.go`):\n- `DB.CleanTombstones()` at lines 2105-2157: Reruns compaction to remove deleted data\n\n**Block Metadata Structure** (`tsdb/block.go`):\n- `BlockMeta` struct at lines 162-212: Contains compaction history and failure flags\n- `BlockMetaCompaction` struct: Tracks compaction level, sources, parents, and failure state\n\n**Metrics Registration** (`tsdb/compact.go`):\n- `NewCompactorMetrics()` at lines 100-151: Registers all compaction metrics\n\n### Key Constants\n\n| Constant | Location | Value | Purpose |\n|----------|----------|-------|---------|\n| `DefaultBlockDuration` | `tsdb/db.go:74` | 2 hours | Head chunk range; minimum block size |\n| `tmpForCreationBlockDirSuffix` | `tsdb/db.go:91` | `.tmp-for-creation` | Atomic write directory for compaction |\n| `tmpForDeletionBlockDirSuffix` | `tsdb/db.go:92` | `.tmp-for-deletion` | Atomic deletion directory |\n| Compaction interval | `tsdb/db.go:1004` | 1 minute | Periodic trigger check frequency |\n| Tombstone threshold | `tsdb/compact.go:323` | 0.05 (5%) | Recompact blocks with >5% tombstones |\n\n### Important Data Structures\n\n**Compactor Interface** (`tsdb/compact.go:59-73`):\n```go\ntype Compactor interface {\n    Plan(dir string) ([]string, error)\n    Write(dest string, b BlockReader, mint, maxt int64, base *BlockMeta) (ulid.ULID, error)\n    Compact(dest string, dirs []string, open []*Block) (ulid.ULID, error)\n}\n```\n\n**CompactorMetrics** (`tsdb/compact.go:89-97`):\n```go\ntype CompactorMetrics struct {\n    Ran               prometheus.Counter      // prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total\n    PopulatingBlocks  prometheus.Gauge        // prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block\n    OverlappingBlocks prometheus.Counter      // prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total\n    Duration          prometheus.Histogram    // prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds\n    ChunkSize         prometheus.Histogram    // prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_size_bytes\n    ChunkSamples      prometheus.Histogram    // prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_samples\n    ChunkRange        prometheus.Histogram    // prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_range_seconds\n}\n```\n\n**Block Compaction Metadata** (`tsdb/block.go:200-212`):\n```go\ntype BlockMetaCompaction struct {\n    Level       int           // Compaction depth\n    Sources     []ulid.ULID   // All source head blocks\n    Deletable   bool          // Mark for deletion\n    Parents     []BlockDesc   // Direct parent blocks\n    Failed      bool          // Compaction failure flag\n    Hints       []string      // Metadata hints\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Operational Best Practices\n\n### Proactive Monitoring Setup\n\n1. **Alert on compaction stall**:\n   ```yaml\n   - alert: TsdbCompactionNotProgressing\n     expr: rate(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total[5m]) == 0\n     for: 10m\n     annotations:\n       summary: \"Prometheus compaction not progressing\"\n   ```\n\n2. **Alert on excessive OOM compactions**:\n   ```yaml\n   - alert: TsdbCompactionOOM\n     expr: increase(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_oom_errors_total[5m]) > 0\n     annotations:\n       summary: \"Compaction OOM errors detected\"\n   ```\n\n3. **Alert on block reload failures**:\n   ```yaml\n   - alert: TsdbReloadsFailed\n     expr: rate(prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total[5m]) > 0\n     annotations:\n       summary: \"TSDB block reload failures\"\n   ```\n\n### Maintenance Windows\n\n- **Monthly block integrity check**:\n  ```bash\n  promtool tsdb list /path/to/prometheus/data\n  promtool tsdb analyze /path/to/prometheus/data <recent_block_ulid>\n  ```\n\n- **Quarterly retention audit**:\n  - Review disk usage vs. retention policy\n  - Adjust block duration if high memory usage during compaction\n  - Verify oldest blocks are being properly deleted\n\n### Retention Policy Tuning\n\nUse this formula to set retention:\n```\nretention_size \u2248 (average_ingestion_rate_Mbps) \u00d7 (retention_days) \u00d7 86400 \u00d7 1.2\n```\n\nExample: 10 Mbps ingestion, 15-day retention:\n```\n10 \u00d7 15 \u00d7 86400 \u00d7 1.2 \u2248 15.5 GB storage needed\n```\n\nConfigure in Prometheus:\n```yaml\nglobal:\n  retention: \"15d\"\n  retention_size: \"16GB\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Additional Resources\n\n### Prometheus Documentation\n- [TSDB Storage Format](https://prometheus.io/docs/prometheus/latest/storage/#tsdb)\n- [Command-line Flags](https://prometheus.io/docs/prometheus/latest/command-line/prometheus/#--storage.tsdb.max-block-duration)\n\n### Debugging Tools\n- `promtool tsdb list` \u2014 List blocks in database\n- `promtool tsdb analyze` \u2014 Analyze block contents and compaction efficiency\n- `promtool tsdb dump` \u2014 Export samples from block\n- `pprof` \u2014 CPU/memory profiling of Prometheus process\n\n### Common Compaction Configurations\n\n**High-Cardinality Environments**:\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  tsdb:\n    max_block_duration: 3h      # Larger blocks reduce compaction frequency\n```\n\n**Memory-Constrained Environments**:\n```yaml\nglobal:\n  retention: \"3d\"               # Shorter retention = fewer blocks to compact\n  retention_size: \"5GB\"         # Hard limit on storage\n```\n\n**High-Write-Volume Environments**:\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  tsdb:\n    out_of_order_time_window: 30m  # Handle out-of-order writes separately\n```\n\n",
